CUDA EGL Plane Descriptor -\/ structure defining each plane of a CUDA EGLFrame \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaccaca30f870ee63d89b579b430422c5f}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaccaca30f870ee63d89b579b430422c5f} 
\index{Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}!cudaEglResourceLocationFlags@{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags}}
\index{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags@{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags}!Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags}{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{typedef}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5f}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags\+\_\+enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaccaca30f870ee63d89b579b430422c5f}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags}}}

Resource location flags-\/ sysmem or vidmem

For CUDA context on i\+GPU, since video and system memory are equivalent -\/ these flags will not have an effect on the execution.

For CUDA context on d\+GPU, applications can use the flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaccaca30f870ee63d89b579b430422c5f}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags} to give a hint about the desired location.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5fa502da824e4d8837a90e09aec82727f9e}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Sysmem} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the system memory to be accessed by CUDA.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5faf3361b86e6f88245861cac54cb58f58e}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Vidmem} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the dedicated video memory to be accessed by CUDA.

There may be an additional latency due to new allocation and data migration, if the frame is produced on a different memory. \Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8d98c18806b2361aeb23e07a3bda96da}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga8d98c18806b2361aeb23e07a3bda96da}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{cudaEglFrameTypePitch@{cudaEglFrameTypePitch}!Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}}\index{Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}!cudaEglFrameTypePitch@{cudaEglFrameTypePitch}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ggabb3a6475fec707b29b3f03c0e786750eaa5abdfca5372c8f235c4a32aa73a1c23}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ggabb3a6475fec707b29b3f03c0e786750eaa5abdfca5372c8f235c4a32aa73a1c23}

\index{Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}!cudaEglResourceLocationFlags\_enum@{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}}
\index{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags\_enum@{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}!Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}{cudaEglResourceLocationFlags\_enum}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{enum}} \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_ga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5f}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags\+\_\+enum}}}

Resource location flags-\/ sysmem or vidmem

For CUDA context on i\+GPU, since video and system memory are equivalent -\/ these flags will not have an effect on the execution.

For CUDA context on d\+GPU, applications can use the flag \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gaccaca30f870ee63d89b579b430422c5f}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Flags} to give a hint about the desired location.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5fa502da824e4d8837a90e09aec82727f9e}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Sysmem} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the system memory to be accessed by CUDA.

\doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5faf3361b86e6f88245861cac54cb58f58e}{cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Vidmem} -\/ the frame data is made resident on the dedicated video memory to be accessed by CUDA.

There may be an additional latency due to new allocation and data migration, if the frame is produced on a different memory. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{cudaEglResourceLocationSysmem@{cudaEglResourceLocationSysmem}!Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}}\index{Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}!cudaEglResourceLocationSysmem@{cudaEglResourceLocationSysmem}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5fa502da824e4d8837a90e09aec82727f9e}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5fa502da824e4d8837a90e09aec82727f9e} 
cuda\+Egl\+Resource\+Location\+Sysmem&Resource location sysmem \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{cudaEglResourceLocationVidmem@{cudaEglResourceLocationVidmem}!Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}}\index{Data types used by CUDA Runtime@{Data types used by CUDA Runtime}!cudaEglResourceLocationVidmem@{cudaEglResourceLocationVidmem}}}\Hypertarget{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5faf3361b86e6f88245861cac54cb58f58e}\label{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_y_p_e_s_gga412bd03963f4da2a1803b30b66286b5faf3361b86e6f88245861cac54cb58f58e}
